 ) Today is the birth anniversary of Yashpal, the well-known storyteller who developed the story-tradition of Premchand
 3 disambar 1903 ko punjab ke ferozepur main unka janm hua
 Literature was such a scripture for Yashpal that he had to win the entire war of culture! And they won! At each level they were alert! Thoughts, arguments, satire, artistic beauty, poignancy - he gave evidence of his genius at every level! Wherever there was exploitation and oppression in the society, wherever in the clutches of stereotypes, traditions, morals, religion and rites It was there, Yashpal's eyesight fell there and he hit it with full force! With this vision, he entered the field of history where his horrific experiences were called grand and divine! He ruined that anti-human history! Yashpal was a great figure of human values, but satire has been like a sword in his creation and he has been a warrior dedicated to the reconstruction of new society! Heartrending vision, Adult thoughts and revolutionary philosophy have placed him among the greatest creators of the world! His representative stories bring evidence of his meteoric journey!  48 saal purana yah kanoon yuddh ke baad pakistan yaa china main bas gaye logon kii chodi hui sampattiyon ke uttaradhikaar yaa hastantaran ke daavon se judaa he
 'enemy property' means any property which belongs to, or is managed on behalf of, any enemy, enemy person or enemy firm
 tippaniyan The bill was passed by the Lok Sabha earlier this year, but it could not get approval from the Rajya Sabha

 bhautik vigyaan ke kshetra main saral aavart gati ko jaananaa bahut jaruri he kyonki saral aavart gati kii sahaayta se hi kisi pind ko samajha jaataa he
 Simple harmonic motion: 1
 aavart gati (periodic motion):ek nishchit path par gati karti vastu jab kisi nishchit samay -antaraal ke pashchaat baar-baar apni purv gati ko doharaati he, to is prakaar kii gati ko aavart gati kehete hai
 2
 dolan gati (oscillatory motion):kisi pind kii samya sthiti ke idhar-udhar karne ko dolan gati yaa companik gati kehete hai
 What is called oscillation- (i) oscillation - a oscillation or a oscillation: The oscillating particle moving to its equilibrium position then moving to the other position and returning to the equilibrium state again, is called a oscillation or oscillation
 
 (ii) aavart kaal (time period):ek dolan puraa karne ke samay ko aavart kaal kehete he
 3
 aavriti (frequency):kampan karne vaali vastu ek second main jitna kampan karti he, use uski aavriti kehete he
 Its s
 I
 The unit is hertz
 yadi aavriti n tathaa aavart kaal t ho, to n = 1 / t hota he
 (i) Simple harmonic motion: If an object moves a moving line around the mean position such that the acceleration of the object is directly proportional to the displacement of the object from the mean position and the direction of acceleration
 If the mean is towards the point, then its motion is called simple period
 saral aavart gati kii visheshtaayen :(i)us par koi bal kaary nahin karata he
 (ii) Its acceleration is zero
 (iii)veg adhiktam hota he
 (iv) The kinetic energy is maximum
 (v)sthitij urja shunya hoti he
 4
 saral aavart gati karne vaala kan jab apni gati ke ant binduon se gujarata he, to(i)uskaa twaran adhiktam hota he
 (ii) The afferent force acting on it is maximum
 (iii) gatij urja shunya hoti he
 (iv) potential energy is maximum
 (v) veg shunya hota he
 5
 saral lolak (simple pendulum):yadi ek bharahin va lambaai main na badhanevaali doli ke nikle sir se padaarth ke kisi gol paratu baari kan ko latakaakar dori ko kisi drudh aadhaar se lataka den to is samaayojan ko 'saral lolak' kehete he
 If the bob is displaced slightly from its equilibrium position, its speed is simple periodic motion
 yadi dori ko prabhavi lambaai l evam gurutveey twaran g ho, tii saral6
 The periodicity of the pendulum is t = 2π √l / g
 isse nimna nishkarsh nikalate he:(i)t ∝ √l, athart lambaai badhane par t bad jayega
 This is the reason that if a girl is standing swinging and swinging, then her center of gravity will rise up and the effective length will decrease which will reduce the swing period
 athart jhula jaldi-jaldi dolan karegaa
 (ii) The periodic period does not depend on the mass of the pendulum, so if the girl of the swinging girl comes and sits, the periodic period will not be affected
 (iii )T = √l / g yani kisi lolak ghadi ko prithvi tal se upar yaa neeche le jaaya jaae to ghadi kaavartkaal (T) bad jaataa he, athart ghadi sust ho jaati he, kyonki prithvi tal se upar yaa neeche par 'g' kaa maan kam hota he
 (iv) If the pendulum is carried on the satellite, then g = 0 due to weightlessness, hence the clock period (T) will go to infinity; So the pendulum clock in the satellite will not work
 7
 In the summer, the length of the pendulum will increase (l), then its periodic (T) will also increase
 atah ghadi sust pad jaaegi
 When the length (l) decreases in winter, the periodic (T) will also increase and the pendulum clock will start running faster
 8
 Carrying a pendulum clock on the moon will increase its periodicity, because the value of g on the moon is 1 / 6 times the value of g on Earth

 supreme court ne saaf kiya ki jo maamle hai court ke saamne lambit hai unamem dakhal nahin denge lekin shahabuddin ko bihar se tihaad jail transfar kiya jaae yaa nahin, is par vichaar jarur karenge
 The cases which are pending in the lower court should be transferred to Delhi or not or will transfer Shahabuddin to Tihar and continue the trial in the lower court
 agar jarurat hogi ho shahabuddin ko video conferencing ke jariye adaalat main pesh kiya ja sakegaa
